      return self.index < self.args.len;\n   894→    }\n   895→\n   896→    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   897→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   898→        return self.args[self.index];\n   899→    }\n   900→\n   901→    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   902→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   903→        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n   904→        self.index += 1;\n   905→        return arg;\n   906→    }\n   907→\n   908→    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n   909→    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n   910→        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n   911→            self.index += 1;\n   912→        }\n   913→    }\n   914→\n   915→    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n   916→    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n   917→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n   918→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n   919→            self.skip();\n   920→            return true;\n   921→        }\n   922→        return false;\n   923→    }\n   924→\n   925→    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n   926→    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   927→        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   928→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   929→    }\n   930→\n   931→    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n   932→    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   933→        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n   934→            return try self.consumeU32();\n   935→        }\n   936→        return null;\n   937→    }\n   938→\n   939→    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n   940→    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   941→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n   942→        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n   943→        return arg;\n   944→    }\n   945→};\n   946→\n   947→// Tests\n print ID only).\n   161→pub fn runQuick(\n   162→    quick_args: args.QuickArgs,\n   163→    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n   164→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   165→) !void {\n   166→    // timestamp.\n   182→/// Supports: YYYY-MM-DD, YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ\n   183→fn parseDateString(date_str: []const u8) ?i64 {\n   184→    // Try RFC3339 format first\n   185→    if (@import(\"../models/timestamp.zig\").parseRfc3339(date_str)) |ts| {\n   186→        return ts;\n   187→    }\n   188→\n   189→    // Try YYYY-MM-DD format\n   190→    if (date_str.len == 10 and date_str[4] == '-' and date_str[7] == '-') {\n   191→        const year = std.fmt.parseInt(i32, date_str[0..4], 10) catch return null;\n   192→        const month = std.fmt.parseInt(u4, date_str[5..7], 10) catch return null;\n   193→        const day = std.fmt.parseInt(u5, date_str[8..10], 10) catch return null;\n   194→\n   195→        if (month < 1 or month > 12) return null;\n   196→        if (day < 1 or day > 31) return null;\n   197→\n   198→        // Convert to days since epoch\n   199→        const epoch_day = epochDayFromYMD(year, month, day) catch return null;\n   200→\n   201→        // Convert to seconds (midnight UTC)\n   202→        return @as(i64, epoch_day) * 86400;\n   203→    }\n   204→\n   205→    return null;\n   206→}\n   207→\n   208→/// Calculate epoch day from year/month/day.\n   209→fn epochDayFromYMD(year: i32, month: u4, day: u5) !i32 {\n   210→    // Algorithm from Howard Hinnant's date algorithms\n   211→    const y: i32 = if (month <= 2) year - 1 else year;\n   212→    const era: i32 = @divTrunc(if (y >= 0) y else y - 399, 400);\n   213→    const yoe: u32 = @intCast(y - era * 400);\n   214→    const m: u32 = month;\n   215→    const doy: u32 = (153 * (if (m > 2) m - 3 else m + 9) + 2) / 5 + day - 1;\n   216→    const doe: u32 = yoe * 365 + yoe / 4 - yoe / 100 + doy;\n   217→    return era * 146097 + @as(i32, @intCast(doe)) - 719468;\n   218→}\n   219→\n   220→/// Get the default actor name from environment.\n   221→/// On Windows, returns null (env var access requires allocation).\n   222→/// Use --actor flag to specify  22→\n    23→/// Context for executing a CLI command with an initialized workspace.\n    24→pub const CommandContext = struct {\n    25→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    26→    output: Output,\n    27→    store: IssueStore,\n    28→    issues_path: []const u8,\n    29→    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    30→\n    31→    /// Initialize a command context by loading the workspace.\n    32→    /// Returns null and outputs an error if workspace is not initialized.\n    33→    pub fn init(\n    34→        allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    35→        global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    36→    ) CommandError!?CommandContext {\n    37→        var output = Output.init(allocator, .{\n    38→            .json = global.json,\n    39→            .toon = global.toon,\n    40→            .quiet =              return CommandError.StorageError;\n    68→            }\n    69→        };\n    70→\n    71→        return CommandContext{\n    72→            .allocator = allocator,\n    73→            .output = output,\n    74→            .store = store,\n    75→            .issues_path = issues_path,\n    76→            .global = global,\n    77→        };\n    78→    }\n    79→\n    80→    /// Clean up resources.\n    81→    pub fn deinit(self: *CommandContext) void {\n    82→        self.store.deinit();\n    83→        self.allocator.free(self.issues_path);\n    84→    }\n    85→\n    86→    /// Save the store to file if auto-flush is enabled.\n    87→    pub fn saveIfAutoFlush(self: *CommandContext) CommandError!void {\n    88→        if (!self.global.no_auto_flush) {\n    89→ appropriate format.\n   103→pub fn outputErrorGeneric(output: *Output, json_mode: bool, message: []const u8) !void {\n   104→    if (json_mode) {\n   105→        try output.printJson(.{\n   106→ CLI COMMAND STRUCTURE\n\n**Dispatch Pattern (main.zig)**\n- Main dispatcher uses a `switch` statement on `result.command` union type\n- Each command case calls `cli.runCommand()` with the specific args type and global options\n- Error handling is done at the dispatch level with `catch |err| switch(err)`\n- Exit codes are set based on error type (e.g., `WorkspaceNotInitialized` -> exit 1)\n\n**Example dispatch pattern:**\n```zig\n.show => |show_args| {\n    cli.runShow(show_args, result.global, allocator) catch |err| switch (err) {\n        error.WorkspaceNotInitialized, error.IssueNotFound => std.process.exit(1),\n        else => return err,\n    };\n},\n```\n\n### 2. COMMAND CONTEXT (src/cli/common.zig)\n\n**CommandContext struct** provides:\n- `allocator` - Memory allocator\n- `output` - Output formatter\n- `store` - IssueStore for CRUD operations\n- `issues_path` - Path to issues.jsonl\n- `global` - GlobalOptions\n\n**Key methods:**\n- `init()` - Loads workspace and creates context (returns `null` if not initialized)\n- `deinit()` - Cleans up resources\n- `saveIfAutoFlush()` - Saves store to file if `--no-auto-flush` not set\n- `createGraph()` - Creates a DependencyGraph for dependency queries\n\n### 5. OUTPUT MODULE (src/output/mod.zig)\n\n**OutputMode enum:**\n- `plain` - No colors, basic text\n- `rich` - ANSI colors (TTY)\n- `json` - JSON output (structured)\n- `quiet` - ID only\n\n**Output methods:**\n- `printIssue(issue)` - Single issue display\n- `printIssueList(issues)` - List of issues\n- `printJson(value)` - Serializes to JSON\n- `print(fmt, args)` - Printf-style formatting\n- `success(fmt, args)` - Green in rich mode\n- `err(fmt, args)` - Red in rich mode, \"error: \" prefix\n- `warn(fmt, args)` - Yellow warning\n- `info(fmt, args)` - Cyan info\n- `raw(text)` - Raw text output\n\n**TTY Detection:**\n- Uses `stdout.isTty()` to determine if colors should be used\n- Respects NO_COLOR env var\n\n### 6. STORAGE LAYER (src/storage/)\n\n**IssueStore struct** in store.zig provides:\n- `insert(issue)` - Add new issue\n- `get(id)` - Fetch issue with embedded relations\n- `getRef(id)` - Fetch issue reference (no relations)\n- `exists(id)` - Check if issue exists\n- `update(id, updates, timestamp)` - Modify fields\n- `delete(id, timestamp)` - Soft delete (tombstone)\n- `list(filters)` - Query with filters\n- `loadFromFile()` / `saveToFile()` - JSONL persistence\n- `addLabel(id, label)` - Add label to issue\n- `createGraph()` - Create dependency graph\n\n**ListFilters struct:**\n- `status`, `priority`, `issue_type`, `assignee`, `label`, `limit`\n- All optional fields\n\n**IssueUpdate struct:**\n- `title`, `description`, `status`, `priority`, `issue_type`, `assignee`\n- Used for partial updates\n\n### 7.       return self.index < self.args.len;\n   894→    }\n   895→\n   896→    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   897→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   898→        return self.args[self.index];\n   899→    }\n   900→\n   901→    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   902→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   903→        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n   904→        self.index += 1;\n   905→        return arg;\n   906→    }\n   907→\n   908→    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n   909→    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n   910→        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n   911→            self.index += 1;\n   912→        }\n   913→    }\n   914→\n   915→    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n   916→    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n   917→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n   918→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n   919→            self.skip();\n   920→            return true;\n   921→        }\n   922→        return false;\n   923→    }\n   924→\n   925→    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n   926→    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   927→        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   928→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   929→    }\n   930→\n   931→    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n   932→    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   933→        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n   934→            return try self.consumeU32();\n   935→        }\n   936→        return null;\n   937→    }\n   938→\n   939→    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n   940→    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   941→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n   942→        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n   943→        return arg;\n   944→    }\n   945→};\n   946→\n   947→// Tests\n   948→\n   949→test \"parse no arguments shows help\" {\n   950→    const args = [_][]const u8{};\n   951→    var parser = ArgParser.init(std.testing.allocator, &args);\n   952→    const result = try parser.parse();\n   953→\n   954→    try std.testing.expect(result.command == .help);\n   955→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?[]const u8, null), result.command.help.topic);\n   956→}\n   957→\n CLI argument parsing for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Parses command-line arguments into structured data for command dispatch.\n//! Supports global flags, subcommands, and subcommand-specific arguments.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\n\n/// Global CLI options that apply to all commands.\npub const GlobalOptions = struct {\n    json: bool = false,\n    toon: bool = false,\n    quiet: bool = false,\n    verbose: u8 = 0,\n    no_color: bool = false,\n    data_path: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    actor: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    lock_timeout: u32 = 5000,\n    no_auto_flush: bool = false,\n    no_auto_import: bool = false,\n\n    /// Returns true if structured output (JSON or TOON) is enabled.\n    pub fn isStructuredOutput(self: GlobalOptions) bool {\n        return self.json or self.toon;\n    }\n};\n\n/// All available subcommands.\npub const Command = union(enum) {\n    // Workspace\n    init: InitArgs,\n    info: void,\n    stats: void,\n    doctor: void,\n    config: ConfigArgs,\n\n    // Issue CRUD\n    create: CreateArgs,\n    q: QuickArgs,\n    show: ShowArgs,\n    update: UpdateArgs,\n    close: CloseArgs,\n    reopen: ReopenArgs,\n    delete: DeleteArgs,\n\n    // Query\n    list: ListArgs,\n    ready: ReadyArgs,\n    blocked: BlockedArgs,\n    search: SearchArgs,\n    stale: StaleArgs,\n    count: CountArgs,\n\n    // Dependencies\n    dep: DepArgs,\n\n    // Labels\n    label: LabelArgs,\n\n    // Comments\n    comments: CommentsArgs,\n\n    // Audit\n    history: HistoryArgs,\n    audit: AuditArgs,\n\n    // Sync\n    sync: SyncArgs,\n\n    // System\n    version: void,\n    schema: void,\n    completions: CompletionsArgs,\n\n    // Help\n    help: HelpArgs,\n};\n\n/// Init command arguments.\npub const InitArgs = struct {\n    prefix: []const u8 = \"bd\",\n};\n\n/// Create command arguments.\npub const CreateArgs = struct {\n    title: []const u8,\n    description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    labels: []const []const u8 = &[_][]const u8{},\n    deps: []const []const u8 = &[_][]const u8{},\n    due: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    estimate: ?i32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Quick capture command arguments.\npub const QuickArgs = struct {\n    title: []const u8,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Show command arguments.\npub const ShowArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Update command arguments.\npub const UpdateArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    status: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Close command arguments.\npub const CloseArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    reason: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Reopen command arguments.\npub const ReopenArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Delete command arguments.\npub const DeleteArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// List command arguments.\npub const ListArgs = struct {\n    status: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    label: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n    all: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Ready command arguments.\npub const ReadyArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Blocked command arguments.\npub const BlockedArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Search command arguments.\npub const SearchArgs = struct {\n    query: []const u8,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Stale command arguments.\npub const StaleArgs = struct {\n    days: u32 = 30,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Count command arguments.\npub const CountArgs = struct {\n    group_by: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Dependency subcommand variants.\npub const DepSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    add: struct {\n        child: []const u8,\n        parent: []const u8,\n        dep_type: []const u8 = \"blocks\",\n    },\n    remove: struct {\n        child: []const u8,\n        parent: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n    tree: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n    cycles: void,\n};\n\n/// Dependency command arguments.\npub const DepArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: DepSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Label subcommand variants.\npub const LabelSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    add: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        labels: []const []const u8,\n    },\n    remove: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        labels: []const []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n    list_all: void,\n};\n\n/// Label command arguments.\npub const LabelArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: LabelSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Comments subcommand variants.\npub const CommentsSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    add: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        text: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n};\n\n/// Comments command arguments.\npub const CommentsArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: CommentsSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// History command arguments.\npub const HistoryArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Audit command arguments.\npub const AuditArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Sync command arguments.\npub const SyncArgs = struct {\n    flush_only: bool = false,\n    import_only: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Shell completion types.\npub const Shell = enum {\n    bash,\n    zsh,\n    fish,\n    powershell,\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?Shell {\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"bash\")) return .bash;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"zsh\")) return .zsh;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"fish\")) return .fish;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"powershell\")) return .powershell;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"ps\")) return .powershell;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Completions command arguments.\npub const CompletionsArgs = struct {\n    shell: Shell,\n};\n\n/// Help command arguments.\npub const HelpArgs = struct {\n    topic: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Config subcommand variants.\npub const ConfigSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    get: struct {\n        key: []const u8,\n    },\n    set: struct {\n        key: []const u8,\n        value: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: void,\n};\n\n/// Config command arguments.\npub const ConfigArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: ConfigSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Result of parsing command-line arguments.\npub const ParseResult = struct {\n    global: GlobalOptions,\n    command: Command,\n\n    /// Free any memory allocated during parsing (labels, deps slices).\n    pub fn deinit(self: *ParseResult, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        switch (self.command) {\n            .create => |create| {\n                if (create.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(create.labels);\n                if (create.deps.len > 0) allocator.free(create.deps);\n            },\n            .label => |label_cmd| {\n                switch (label_cmd.subcommand) {\n                    .add => |add| if (add.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(add.labels),\n                    .remove => |remove| if (remove.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(remove.labels),\n                    else => {},\n                }\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// Errors that can occur during argument parsing.\npub const ParseError = error{\n    UnknownCommand,\n    MissingRequiredArgument,\n    InvalidArgument,\n    UnknownFlag,\n    MissingFlagValue,\n    InvalidShell,\n    UnknownSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Command-line argument parser.\npub const ArgParser = struct {\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    args: []const []const u8,\n    index: usize = 0,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, args: []const []const u8) Self {\n        return .{\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .args = args,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse all arguments into a ParseResult.\n    pub fn parse(self: *Self) ParseError!ParseResult {\n        var global = GlobalOptions{};\n\n        // Parse global flags first\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            const arg = self.peek().?;\n            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) {\n                if (self.parseGlobalFlag(&global)) |consumed| {\n                    if (!consumed) break;\n                } else |_| {\n                    break;\n                }\n            } else {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Parse subcommand\n        const cmd_str = self.next() orelse {\n            return .{\n                .global = global,\n                .command = .{ .help = .{ .topic = null } },\n            };\n        };\n\n        const command = try self.parseCommand(cmd_str);\n\n        return .{\n            .global = global,\n            .command = command,\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn parseGlobalFlag(self: *Self, global: *GlobalOptions) ParseError!bool {\n        const arg = self.next().?;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--json\")) {\n            global.json = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--toon\")) {\n            global.toon = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--quiet\")) {\n            global.quiet = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-v\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--verbose\")) {\n            global.verbose +|= 1;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-vv\")) {\n            global.verbose +|= 2;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-color\")) {\n            global.no_color = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-flush\")) {\n            global.no_auto_flush = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-import\")) {\n            global.no_auto_import = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--data\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--db\")) {\n            global.data_path = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--actor\")) {\n            global.actor = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--lock-timeout\")) {\n            const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            global.lock_timeout = std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        // Put back if not recognized\n        self.index -= 1;\n        return error.UnknownFlag;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCommand(self: *Self, cmd: []const u8) ParseError!Command {\n        // Workspace\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"init\")) {\n            return .{ .init = try self.parseInitArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"info\")) {\n            return .{ .info = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"stats\")) {\n            return .{ .stats = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"doctor\")) {\n            return .{ .doctor = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"config\")) {\n            return .{ .config = try self.parseConfigArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Issue CRUD\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"create\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"new\")) {\n            return .{ .create = try self.parseCreateArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"quick\")) {\n            return .{ .q = try self.parseQuickArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"show\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"get\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"view\")) {\n            return .{ .show = try self.parseShowArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"update\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"edit\")) {\n            return .{ .update = try self.parseUpdateArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"close\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"done\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"finish\")) {\n            return .{ .close = try self.parseCloseArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"reopen\")) {\n            return .{ .reopen = try self.parseReopenArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"delete\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"rm\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"remove\")) {\n            return .{ .delete = try self.parseDeleteArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Query\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .list = try self.parseListArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ready\")) {\n            return .{ .ready = try self.parseReadyArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"blocked\")) {\n            return .{ .blocked = try self.parseBlockedArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"search\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"find\")) {\n            return .{ .search = try self.parseSearchArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"stale\")) {\n            return .{ .stale = try self.parseStaleArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"count\")) {\n            return .{ .count = try self.parseCountArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Dependencies\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"dep\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"deps\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"dependency\")) {\n            return .{ .dep = try self.parseDepArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Labels\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"label\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"labels\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"tag\")) {\n            return .{ .label = try self.parseLabelArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Comments\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"comments\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"comment\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"note\")) {\n            return .{ .comments = try self.parseCommentsArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Audit\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"history\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"log\")) {\n            return .{ .history = try self.parseHistoryArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"audit\")) {\n            return .{ .audit = try self.parseAuditArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Sync\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"sync\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"flush\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"export\")) {\n            return .{ .sync = try self.parseSyncArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // System\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"version\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--version\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-V\")) {\n            return .{ .version = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"schema\")) {\n            return .{ .schema = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completions\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completion\")) {\n            return .{ .completions = try self.parseCompletionsArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Help\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-h\")) {\n            return .{ .help = try self.parseHelpArgs() };\n        }\n\n        return error.UnknownCommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseInitArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!InitArgs {\n        var result = InitArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--prefix\")) {\n                result.prefix = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                result.prefix = self.next().?;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCreateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CreateArgs {\n        var result = CreateArgs{ .title = undefined };\n        var title_set = false;\n        var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        var deps: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"--depends-on\", \"--dep\")) {\n                deps.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--due\")) {\n                result.due = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-e\", \"--estimate\")) {\n                const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.estimate = std.fmt.parseInt(i32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!title_set) {\n                    result.title = self.next().?;\n                    title_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!title_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (labels.items.len > 0) {\n            result.labels = labels.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n        }\n        if (deps.items.len > 0) {\n            result.deps = deps.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n        }\n\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseQuickArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!QuickArgs {\n        var result = QuickArgs{ .title = undefined };\n        var title_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!title_set) {\n                    result.title = self.next().?;\n                    title_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!title_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseShowArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ShowArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseUpdateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!UpdateArgs {\n        var result = UpdateArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--title\")) {\n                result.title = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-s\", \"--status\")) {\n                result.status = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!id_set) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                    id_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!id_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCloseArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CloseArgs {\n        var result = CloseArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-r\", \"--reason\")) {\n                result.reason = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!id_set) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                    id_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!id_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseReopenArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ReopenArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseDeleteArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!DeleteArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseListArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ListArgs {\n        var result = ListArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-s\", \"--status\")) {\n                result.status = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n                result.label = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-A\", \"--all\")) {\n                result.all = true;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseReadyArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ReadyArgs {\n        var result = ReadyArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseBlockedArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!BlockedArgs {\n        var result = BlockedArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseSearchArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!SearchArgs {\n        var result = SearchArgs{ .query = undefined };\n        var query_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!query_set) {\n                    result.query = self.next().?;\n                    query_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!query_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseStaleArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!StaleArgs {\n        var result = StaleArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--days\")) {\n                result.days = try self.consumeU32() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCountArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CountArgs {\n        var result = CountArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-g\", \"--group-by\")) {\n                result.group_by = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseDepArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!DepArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\")) {\n            const child = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const parent = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            var dep_type: []const u8 = \"blocks\";\n            while (self.hasNext()) {\n                if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                    dep_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                } else break;\n            }\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .child = child, .parent = parent, .dep_type = dep_type } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const child = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const parent = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .child = child, .parent = parent } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"tree\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .tree = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"cycles\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .cycles = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseLabelArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!LabelArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const is_add = std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\");\n            const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n\n            while (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next().?) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            }\n\n            if (labels.items.len == 0) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n            const label_slice = labels.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            if (is_add) {\n                return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .id = id, .labels = label_slice } } };\n            } else {\n                return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .id = id, .labels = label_slice } } };\n            }\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list-all\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"all\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list_all = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCommentsArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CommentsArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{\n                .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n                .text = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n            } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseHistoryArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!HistoryArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseAuditArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!AuditArgs {\n        var result = AuditArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseSyncArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!SyncArgs {\n        var result = SyncArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"--export\", \"--flush-only\")) {\n                result.flush_only = true;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"--import\", \"--import-only\")) {\n                result.import_only = true;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCompletionsArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CompletionsArgs {\n        const shell_str = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        const shell = Shell.fromString(shell_str) orelse return error.InvalidShell;\n        return .{ .shell = shell };\n    }\n\n    fn parseHelpArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!HelpArgs {\n        return .{ .topic = self.next() };\n    }\n\n    fn parseConfigArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ConfigArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = {} } };\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"get\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .get = .{ .key = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"set\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .set = .{\n                .key = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n                .value = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n            } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn hasNext(self: *Self) bool {\n        return self.index < self.args.len;\n    }\n\n    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n        return self.args[self.index];\n    }\n\n    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n        self.index += 1;\n        return arg;\n    }\n\n    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n            self.index += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n            self.skip();\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n            return try self.consumeU32();\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n        return arg;\n    }\n};\n\n// Tests\n\ntest \"parse no arguments shows help\" {\n    const args = [_][]const u8{};\n    var parser = ArgParser.init(std.testing.allocator, &args);\n    const result = try parser.parse();\n\n    try std.testing.expect(result.command == .help);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?[]const u8, null), result.command.help.topic);\n}\n\ntest 151→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   152→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   153→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   154→    }\n   155→\n   156→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout with newline.\n   157→    pub fn println(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   158→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   159→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt ++ \"\\n\", args);\n   160→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   161→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   162→    }\n   163→\n   164→    /// Print a success message (green in rich mode).\n   165→    pub fn success(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   166→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   167→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.green);\n   168→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   169→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   170→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   171→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   172→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   173→    }\n   174→\n   175→    /// Print an error message to stderr (red in rich mode).\n   176→    pub fn err(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   177→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.red);\n   178→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"error: \" ++ fmt, args);\n   179→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   180→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   181→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   182→        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   183→    }\n   184→\n   185→    /// Print a warning message to stderr (yellow in rich mode).\n   186→    pub fn warn(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   187→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   188→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.yellow);\n   189→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"warning: \" ++ fmt, args);\n   190→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   191→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   192→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   193→        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   194→    }\n   195→\n   196→    /// Print an info message (cyan in rich mode).\n   197→    pub fn info(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   198→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   199→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.cyan);\n   200→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   201→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   202→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   203→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   204→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   205→    }\n   206→\n   207→    /// Print raw bytes to stdout (bypasses mode checks).\n   208→    pub fn raw(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) !void {\n   209→        try self.stdout.writeAll(bytes);\n   210→    }\n   211→\n   212→    /// Print raw JSON value to stdout (for JSON mode).\n   213→    /// If toon mode is enabled, converts JSON to TOON format for reduced token usage.\n   214→    pub fn printJson(self: *Self, value: anytype) !void {\n   215→        const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, value, .{});\n   216→        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   217→\n   218→        if (self.toon) {\n   219→            const toon = @import(\"toon_zig\");\n   220→            const toon_bytes = toon.jsonToToon(self.allocator, json_bytes) catch |convert_err| {\n   221→                try self.stderr.writeAll(\"error: failed to convert to TOON format\\n\");\n   222→                return convert_err;\n   223→            };\n   224→            defer self.allocator.free(toon_bytes);\n   225→            try self.stdout.writeAll(toon_bytes);\n   226→        } else {\n   227→            try self.stdout.writeAll(json_bytes);\n   228→        }\n   229→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   230→    }\n   231→\n   232→    // ========================================================================\n   233→    // JSON Mode Helpers\n   234→    // ========================================================================\n   235→\n   236→    fn printIssueJson(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   237→        try self.printJson(issue);\n   238→    }\n   239→\n   240→    fn printIssueListJson(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   241→        try self.printJson(issues);\n   242→    }\n   243→\n   244→    // ========================================================================\n   245→    // Plain Mode Helpers\n   246→    // ========================================================================\n   247→\n   248→    fn printIssuePlain(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   249→        try self.writeFormatted(\"ID: {s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   250→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Title: {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   251→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Status: {s}\\n\", .{issue.status.toString()});\n   252→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Priority: {s}\\n\", .{issue.priority.toString()});\n   253→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   254→\n   255→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   256→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Description: {s}\\n\", .{desc});\n   257→        }\n   258→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   259→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Assignee: {s}\\n\", .{assignee});\n   260→        }\n   261→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   262→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"Labels: \");\n   263→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   264→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   265→                try self.stdout.writeAll(label);\n   266→            }\n   267→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   268→        }\n   269→        if (issue.due_at.value) |due| {\n   270→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Due: {d}\\n\", .{due});\n   271→        }\n   272→\n   273→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Created: {d}\\n\", .{issue.created_at.value});\n   274→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Updated: {d}\\n\", .{issue.updated_at.value});\n   275→    }\n   276→\n   277→    fn printIssueListPlain(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   278→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   279→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   280→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}  [{s}] {s}\\n\", .{\n   281→                issue.id,\n   282→                status_abbrev,\n   283→                issue.title,\n   284→            });\n   285→        }\n   286→    }\n   287→\n   288→    // ========================================================================\n   289→    // Rich Mode Helpers (ANSI colors)\n   290→    // ========================================================================\n   291→\n   292→    fn printIssueRich(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   293→        // Bold ID\n   294→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.bold, issue.id, Color.reset });\n   295→\n   296→        // Title\n   297→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   298→\n   299→        // Status with color\n   300→        const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   301→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Status: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ status_color, issue.status.toString(), Color.reset });\n   302→\n   303→        // Priority with color\n   304→        const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   305→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Priority: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ priority_color, issue.priority.toString(), Color.reset });\n   306→\n   307→        // Type\n   308→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   309→\n   310→        // Optional fields\n   311→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   312→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Description: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.dim, desc, Color.reset });\n   313→        }\n   314→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   315→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Assignee: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.cyan, assignee, Color.reset });\n   316→        }\n   317→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   318→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"  Labels: \");\n   319→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   320→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   321→                try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\", .{ Color.magenta, label, Color.reset });\n   322→            }\n   323→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   324→        }\n   325→    }\n   326→\n   327→    fn printIssueListRich(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   328→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   329→            const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   330→            const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   331→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   332→\n   333→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}  {s}[{s}]{s}  {s}{s}{s}  {s}\\n\", .{\n   334→                Color.bold,\n   335→                issue.id,\n   336→                Color.reset,\n   337→                status_color,\n   338→                status_abbrev,\n   339→                Color.reset,\n   340→                priority_color,\n   341→                priorityIndicator(issue.priority),\n   342→                Color.reset,\n   343→                issue.title,\n   344→            });\n   345→        }\n   346→    }\n   347→\n   348→    // ========================================================================\n   349→    // Quiet Mode Helpers\n   350→    // ========================================================================\n   351→\n   352→    fn printIssueQuiet(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   353→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   354→    }\n   355→\n   356→    fn printIssueListQuiet(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   357→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   358→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   359→        }\n   360→    }\n   361→\n   362→    // ========================================================================\n   363→    // Internal Helpers\n   364→    // ========================================================================\n   365→\n   366→    fn writeFormatted(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   367→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   368→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   369→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   370→    }\n   371→};\n   372→\n   373→// ============================================================================\n   374→// Helper Functions\n   375→// ============================================================================\n   376→\n   377→/// Check if NO_COLOR environment variable is set (cross-platform).\n   378→fn checkNoColorEnv() bool {\n   379→    // Per NO_COLOR spec, only existence matters, not the value\n   380→    return std.process.hasEnvVarConstant(\"NO_COLOR\");\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→/// Get ANSI color for a status.\n   384→fn getStatusColor(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   385→    return switch (status) {\n   386→        .open => Color.green,\n   387→        .in_progress => Color.yellow,\n   388→        .blocked => Color.red,\n   389→        .deferred => Color.gray,\n   390→        .closed => Color.gray,\n   391→        .tombstone => Color.dim,\n   392→        .pinned => Color.bright_cyan,\n   393→        .custom => Color.blue,\n   394→    };\n   395→}\n   396→\n   397→/// Get ANSI color for a priority.\n   398→fn getPriorityColor(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   399→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   400→        0 => Color.bright_red, // critical\n   401→        1 => Color.red, // high\n   402→        2 => Color.yellow, // medium\n   403→        3 => Color.green, // low\n   404→        4 => Color.gray, // backlog\n   405→        else => Color.reset,\n   406→    };\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→/// Get short status abbreviation.\n   410→fn abbreviateStatus(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   411→    return switch (status) {\n   412→        .open => \"OPEN\",\n   413→        .in_progress => \"PROG\",\n   414→        .blocked => \"BLKD\",\n   415→        .deferred => \"DEFR\",\n   416→        .closed => \"DONE\",\n   417→        .tombstone => \"DEL \",\n   418→        .pinned => \"PIN \",\n   419→        .custom => \"CUST\",\n   420→    };\n   421→}\n   422→\n   423→/// Get priority indicator symbol.\n   424→fn priorityIndicator(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   425→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   426→        0 => \"!!!\",\n   427→        1 => \"!! \",\n   428→        2 => \"!  \",\n   429→        3 => \".  \",\n   430→        4 => \"   \",\n   431→        else => \"   \",\n   432→    };\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→// ============================================================================\n   436→// Tests\n   437→// ============================================================================\n   438→\n   439→test \"OutputMode enum values\" {\n   440→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, OutputMode.plain);\n   441→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, OutputMode.rich);\n   442→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, OutputMode.json);\n   443→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, OutputMode.quiet);\n   444→}\n   445→\n   446→test \"Output.init with json option\" {\n   447→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   448→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .json = true };\n   449→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   450→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   451→    try std.testing.expect(!output.toon);\n   452→}\n   453→\n   454→test \"Output.init with toon option\" {\n   455→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   456→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .toon = true };\n   457→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   458→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   459→    try std.testing.expect(output.toon);\n   460→}\n   461→\n   462→test \"Output.init with quiet option\" {\n   463→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   464→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .quiet = true };\n   465→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   466→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, output.mode);\n   467→}\n   468→\n   469→test \"Output.init with no_color option forces plain mode\" {\n   470→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   471→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .no_color = true };\n   472→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   473→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, output.mode);\n   474→}\n   475→\n   476→test \"Output.init json overrides quiet\" {\n   477→    const std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   481→}\n   482→\n   483→test \"Output.initWithMode sets explicit mode\" {\n   484→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   485→    const output = Output.initWithMode(allocator, .rich);\n   486→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, output.mode);\n   487→}\n   488→\n   489→test \"abbreviateStatus returns 4-char strings\" {\n   490→    const statuses = [_]Status{\n   491→        .open,\n   492→        .in_progress,\n   493→        .blocked,\n   494→        .deferred,\n   495→        .closed,\n   496→        .tombstone,\n   497→        .pinned,\n   498→        .{ .custom = \"test\" },\n   499→    };\n   500→    for (statuses) |status| {\n   501→        const abbrev = abbreviateStatus(status);\n   502→        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 4), abbrev.len);\n   503→    }\n   504→}\n   505→\n   506→test \"priorityIndicator returns 3-char strings\" {\n   507→    var p: u3 = 0;\n   508→    while (p <= 4) : (p += 1) {\n   509→        const priority = Priority{ .value = p };\n   510→        const indicator = priorityIndicator(priority);\n   511→        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), indicator.len);\n   512→    }\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→test \"getStatusColor returns valid ANSI codes\" {\n   516→    const statuses = [_]Status{\n   517→        .open,\n   518→        .in_progress,\n   519→        .blocked,\n   520→        .deferred,\n   521→        .closed,\n   522→        .tombstone,\n   523→        .pinned,\n   524→        .{ .custom = \"test\" },\n   525→    };\n   526→    for (statuses) |status| {\n   527→        const color = getStatusColor(status);\n   528→        try std.testing.expect(color.len > 0);\n   529→        try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   530→    }\n   531→}\n   532→\n   533→test \"getPriorityColor returns valid ANSI codes\" {\n   534→    var p: u3 = 0;\n   535→    while (p <= 4) : (p += 1) {\n   536→        const priority = Priority{ .value = p };\n   537→        const color = getPriorityColor(priority);\n   538→        try std.testing.expect(color.len > 0);\n   539→        try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   540→    }\n   541→}\n   542→\n   543→test \"Color constants are valid ANSI escape sequences\" {\n   544→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.reset, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   545→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.bold, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   546→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.red, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   547→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.green, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   548→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.yellow, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   549→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.blue, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   550→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.gray, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   551→}\n   552→\n   553→test \"Output printIssueListQuiet writes IDs only\" {\n   554→    // Test the quiet formatting logic directly\n   555→    const issue1 = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue 1\", 1706540000);\n   556→    const issue2 = Issue.init(\"bd-def456\", \"Test issue 2\", 1706540000);\n   557→    const issues = [_]Issue{ issue1, issue2 };\n   558→\n   559→    // In quiet mode, printIssueListQuiet outputs \"{id}\\n\" for each issue\n   560→    // Verify the expected output format\n   561→    try issues.len);\n   564→}\n   565→\n   566→test \"Output printIssueListPlain writes formatted lines\" {\n   567→    // Test the plain formatting logic via abbreviateStatus and Issue fields\n   568→ 576→    const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   577→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"OPEN\", status_abbrev);\n   578→}\n   579→\n   580→test \"Output printIssueListRich includes ANSI codes\" {\n   581→    // Test that rich mode formatting uses ANSI codes\n   582→    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue\", 1706540000);\n   583→\n   584→    // Verify issue fields\n   585→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue.id);\n   586→\n   587→    // Verify rich mode uses color codes\n   588→    const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   589→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, status_color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   590→\n   591→    const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   592→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, priority_color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   593→\n   594→    // Verify Color.bold is used\n   595→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.bold, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   596→}\n   597→\n   598→test \"Output printIssueListJson produces valid JSON array\" {\n   599→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   600→\n   601→    // Test JSON serialization directly\n   602→    const issue1 = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue 1\", 1706540000);\n   603→    const issue2 = Issue.init(\"bd-def456\", \"Test issue 2\", 1706540000);\n   604→    const issues = [_]Issue{ issue1, issue2 };\n   605→\n   606→    // Serialize to JSON\n   607→    const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(allocator, issues, .{});\n   608→    defer allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   609→\n   610→    // Verify it starts with [ and contains expected data\n   611→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, json_bytes, \"[\"));\n   612→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, json_bytes, \"bd-abc123\") != null);\n   613→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, json_bytes, \"bd-def456\") != null);\n   614→\n   615→    // Verify it can be parsed back\n   616→    const parsed = try std.json.parseFromSlice([]const Issue, allocator, json_bytes, .{});\n   617→    defer parsed.deinit();\n   618→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), parsed.value.len);\n   619→}\n   620→\n   621→test \"Output.err formats error messages correctly\" {\n   622→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n allocator.free(msg);\n   627→\n   628→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, msg, \"error:\") != null);\n   629→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, msg, \"test error\") != null);\n   630→}\n   631→\n   632→test \"Output.warn formats warning messages correctly\" {\n   633→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   634→\n   635→    // Test the warning message formatting\n   636→    const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"warning: \" ++ \"this is a warning: {s}\", .{\"be careful\"});\n   637→    defer allocator.free(msg);\n   638→\n   639→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, msg, \"warning:\") != null);\n   640→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, msg, \"be careful\") != null);\n   641→}\n   642→\n   643→test \"Output quiet mode suppresses print but not err\" {\n   644→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   645→\n   646→    // Test quiet mode behavior through Output struct logic\n   647→    const output = Output.initWithMode(allocator, .quiet);\n   648→\n   649→    // Verify quiet mode is set\n   650→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, output.mode);\n   651→\n   652→    // The print/println/success/warn methods check mode == .quiet and return early\n   653→    // The err method does NOT check for quiet mode (always prints)\n   654→    // This is the documented behavior we're testing\n   655→}\n   656→\n   657→test \"Output.success uses green color in rich mode\" {\n   658→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   659→\n   660→    // Test that success would use green color in rich mode\n   661→    const output = Output.initWithMode(allocator, .rich);\n   662→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, output.mode);\n   663→\n   664→    // Verify Color.green is a valid ANSI escape\n   665→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.green, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   666→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.reset, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   667→}\n   668→\n   669→test \"Output.printIssue in plain mode shows all fields\" {\n   670→    // Test issue field access and formatting\n   671→    var issue = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue title\", 1706540000);\n   672→    issue.description = \"A test description\";\n   673→    issue.assignee = \"alice@example.com\";\n   674→\n   675→    // Verify Respects NO_COLOR environment variable and --no-color flag.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst models = @import(\"../models/mod.zig\");\nconst Issue = models.Issue;\nconst Status = {\n    pub const reset = \"\\x1b[0m\";\n    pub const bold = \"\\x1b[1m\";\n    pub const dim = \"\\x1b[2m\";\n    pub const italic = \"\\x1b[3m\";\n    pub const underline = \"\\x1b[4m\";\n\n    pub = \"\\x1b[36m\";\n    pub const white = \"\\x1b[37m\";\n    pub const gray = \"\\x1b[90m\";\n\n    pub const bright_red = \"\\x1b[91m\";\n    pub const bright_green = \"\\x1b[92m\";\n    pub const bright_yellow = \"\\x1b[93m\";\n    pub const bright_blue = \"\\x1b[94m\";\n    pub const bright_magenta = \"\\x1b[95m\";\n    pub const bright_cyan = \"\\x1b[96m\";\n\n    pub const bg_red = \"\\x1b[41m\";\n    pub const bg_green = \"\\x1b[42m\";\n    pub const bg_yellow = \"\\x1b[43m\";\n    pub const bg_blue = \"\\x1b[44m\";\n};\n\n/// Global options that affect output formatting.\n/// This mirrors the relevant fields from cli.args.GlobalOptions.\npub const OutputOptions = struct {\n    json: bool = false,\n    toon: bool = false,\n    quiet: bool = false,\n    no_color: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Output formatter for consistent CLI output across all modes.\npub const Output = struct {\n    mode: OutputMode,\n    toon: bool,\n    stdout: std.fs.File,\n    stderr: std.fs.File,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Initialize output formatter based on global options and TTY detection.\n    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, opts: OutputOptions) Self {\n        const stdout = std.fs.File.stdout();\n        const stderr = std.fs.File.stderr();\n\n        var mode: OutputMode = .plain;\n        if (opts.json or opts.toon) {\n            mode = .json;\n        } else if (opts.quiet) {\n            mode = .quiet;\n        } else if (!opts.no_color and !checkNoColorEnv() and stdout.isTty()) {\n            mode = .rich;\n        }\n\n        return .{\n            .mode = mode,\n            .toon = opts.toon,\n            .stdout = stdout,\n            .stderr = stderr,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Initialize with explicit mode (useful for testing).\n    pub fn initWithMode(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode) Self {\n        return .{\n            .mode = mode,\n            .toon = false,\n            .stdout = std.fs.File.stdout(),\n            .stderr = std.fs.File.stderr(),\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Initialize for testing with custom file handles.\n    pub fn initForTesting(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode, stdout: std.fs.File, stderr: std.fs.File) Self {\n        return .{\n            .mode = mode,\n            .toon = false,\n            .stdout = stdout,\n            .stderr = stderr,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Issue Display\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    /// Print a single issue in the appropriate format.\n    pub fn printIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        switch (self.mode) {\n            .json => try self.printIssueJson(issue),\n            .quiet => try self.printIssueQuiet(issue),\n            .rich => try self.printIssueRich(issue),\n            .plain => try self.printIssuePlain(issue),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Print a list of issues in the appropriate format.\n    pub fn printIssueList(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        switch (self.mode) {\n            .json => try self.printIssueListJson(issues),\n            .quiet => try self.printIssueListQuiet(issues),\n            .rich => try self.printIssueListRich(issues),\n            .plain => try self.printIssueListPlain(issues),\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Generic Messages\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    /// Print a formatted message to stdout.\n    pub fn print(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n    }\n\n    /// Print a formatted message to stdout with newline.\n    pub fn println(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt ++ \"\\n\", args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n    }\n\n    /// Print a success message (green in rich mode).\n    pub fn success(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.green);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// Print an error message to stderr (red in rich mode).\n    pub fn err(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.red);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"error: \" ++ fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    /// Print an info message (cyan in rich mode).\n    pub fn info(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.cyan);\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n        if (self.mode == .rich) try {\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(bytes);\n    }\n\n    /// Print raw JSON value to stdout (for JSON mode).\n    /// If toon mode is enabled, converts JSON to TOON format for reduced token usage.\n    pub fn printJson(self: *Self, value: anytype) !void {\n        const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, value, .{});\n        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n\n        if (self.toon) {\n            const toon = @import(\"toon_zig\");\n            const toon_bytes = toon.jsonToToon(self.allocator, json_bytes) catch |convert_err| {\n                try self.stderr.writeAll(\"error: failed to convert to TOON format\\n\");\n                return convert_err;\n            };\n            defer self.allocator.free(toon_bytes);\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(toon_bytes);\n        } else {\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(json_bytes);\n        }\n        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n\n    // printIssueJson(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.printJson(issue);\n    }\n\n    fn printIssueListJson(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        try      try self.writeFormatted(\"Title: {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Status: {s}\\n\", .{issue.status.toString()});\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"Priority: self.writeFormatted(\"Description: {s}\\n\", .{desc});\n        }\n        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"Assignee: {s}\\n\", .{assignee});\n        }\n          try self.stdout.writeAll(label);\n            }\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n        }\n        if (issue.due_at.value) |due| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"Due: }\n\n    fn printIssueListPlain(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}  [{s}] {s}\\n\", .{\n                issue.id,\n                status_abbrev,\n                issue.title,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Rich Mode Helpers (ANSI colors)\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn printIssueRich(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        // Bold ID\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.bold, issue.id, Color.reset });\n\n        // Title\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n\n        // Status with color\n        const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Status: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ status_color, issue.status.toString(), Color.reset });\n\n        // Priority with color\n        const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Priority: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ priority_color, issue.priority.toString(), Color.reset });\n\n        // Type\n        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n\n        // Optional fields\n        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Description: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.dim, desc, Color.reset });\n        }\n        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Assignee: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.cyan, assignee, Color.reset });\n        }\n        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"  Labels: \");\n            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n                try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\", .{ Color.magenta, label, Color.reset });\n            }\n            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn printIssueListRich(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n            const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n\n            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}  {s}[{s}]{s}  {s}{s}{s}  {s}\\n\", .{\n priority_color,\n                priorityIndicator(issue.priority),\n                Color.reset,\n                issue.title,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Quiet Mode Helpers\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    fn
